Shape 11: If my current ocean carrier has what you outlined in the process flow diagram, I would not switch. It all depends on how much volume you move import/export and the timeliness of updates. How critical is the on-time delivery status.
Also, I might consider using the PF over others, if they provide option A and C with excellent data and timing of the updates.
If you have multiple port stops and long-haul freight to the destination, it's important to predict the arrival to all future destinations.
If you are shipping across the country, acceptable margin error of schedule would be around 7 days +/- 2 days.
Shape 12: My expectation is that the basic information should be available from any logistics service provider so it is definitely useful but I don窶冲 see it as a competitive advantage.
All three options would be useful information, item C is probably the most critical for customer service but A & B would be useful as they would enable operational efficiency. These options would provide competitive advantage vs other service providers
